## **详细描述**<a name="section219756427083931"></a>

显示模块驱动接口定义。

提供给图形系统使用的驱动接口，包括图层管理、设备控制、图形硬件加速、显示内存管理和回调接口等。

**Since：**

1.0

**Version：**

2.0

## **类型定义说明**<a name="section658052615091459"></a>

## HotPlugCallback<a name="ga859a6f8dfa6f6cb04339d1b4f0721ec5"></a>

```
typedef void(* HotPlugCallback) (uint32_t devId, bool connected, void *data)
```

**描述：**

热插拔事件回调。

当有热插拔事件发生时，会回调该接口，需要通过RegHotPlugCallback注册该回调接口。

@paramdevId 输入参数，显示设备ID，此ID由HDI实现层生成，并通过当前回调接口传递给图形服务使用，用以标记当前连接的显示设备。

**参数：**

<a name="table807410534091459"></a>
<table><thead align="left"><tr id="row1044893356091459"><th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.1"><p id="p1590293581091459"><a name="p1590293581091459"></a><a name="p1590293581091459"></a>名称</p>
</th>
<th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.2"><p id="p1311004602091459"><a name="p1311004602091459"></a><a name="p1311004602091459"></a>描述</p>
</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody><tr id="row1269798370091459"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry668635818091459p0"><a name="entry668635818091459p0"></a><a name="entry668635818091459p0"></a>connected</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry1784356729091459p0"><a name="entry1784356729091459p0"></a><a name="entry1784356729091459p0"></a>输入参数，指明设备的连接状态，ture代表连接，false代表断开。</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="row776995200091459"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry965081801091459p0"><a name="entry965081801091459p0"></a><a name="entry965081801091459p0"></a>data</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry846787151091459p0"><a name="entry846787151091459p0"></a><a name="entry846787151091459p0"></a>输出参数，图形服务携带的私有数据，该参数携带的是RegHotPlugCallback接口注册时传递的私有数据地址，详情参考 {@RegHotPlugCallback} 接口注册时传递的地址。</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## RefreshCallback<a name="ga830c7c7818eb9c870bac5d036664ea7e"></a>

```
typedef void(* RefreshCallback) (uint32_t devId, void *data)
```

**描述：**

刷新请求回调。

刷新请求回调，当接口实现层需要图形服务刷新数据帧时会回调该接口，需要通过RegDisplayRefreshCallback注册该回调接口。

**参数：**

**描述：**

<table><thead align="left"><tr id="row1869738830083931"><th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.1"><p id="p1012507407083931"><a name="p1012507407083931"></a><a name="p1012507407083931"></a>枚举值</p>

## MirrorType<a name="ga08d32376574b541d162d8534adb78fd0"></a>

```
enum MirrorType
```

**描述：**

## PixelFormat<a name="ga60883d4958a60b91661e97027a85072a"></a>

## PresentTimestampType<a name="gabdba71665ea5ba4004ac1a9fbeb505f3"></a>

```
enum PresentTimestampType
```

**描述：**

上屏时间戳类型枚举值。

<a name="table1801251507083931"></a>
<table><thead align="left"><tr id="row1944439882083931"><th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.1"><p id="p30891689083931"><a name="p30891689083931"></a><a name="p30891689083931"></a>枚举值</p>
</th>
<th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.2"><p id="p76860278083931"><a name="p76860278083931"></a><a name="p76860278083931"></a>描述</p>
</th>
</tr>

## RopType<a name="ga24265f7618fbdba53d3da4806d3097c4"></a>

```
enum RopType
```

**描述：**

硬件加速支持的ROP操作类型。

硬件加速支持的ROP操作类型，在将前景位图的RGB颜色分量和Alpha分量值与背景位图的RGB颜色 分量值和Alpha分量值进行按位的布尔运算（包括按位与，按位或等），将结果输出。

## TransformType<a name="gaa65f3b21a9a92ff022e435a7304126d2"></a>

```
enum TransformType
```

**描述：**

图层变换类型定义。

<a name="table1778091918083931"></a>

## **函数说明**<a name="section2041776006083931"></a>

## DeviceInitialize\(\)<a name="ga3aba41189809d78958bc6f5cdcee6e56"></a>

```
int32_t DeviceInitialize (DeviceFuncs ** funcs)
```

**描述：**

实现显示设备控制接口的初始化，申请操作显示设备控制接口的资源，并获取对应的操作接口。

**参数：**

<a name="table508771581083931"></a>
<table><thead align="left"><tr id="row610472807083931"><th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.1"><p id="p817429034083931"><a name="p817429034083931"></a><a name="p817429034083931"></a>名称</p>
</th>
<th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.2"><p id="p1782047711083931"><a name="p1782047711083931"></a><a name="p1782047711083931"></a>描述</p>
</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody><tr id="row119782823083931"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry1381994375083931p0"><a name="entry1381994375083931p0"></a><a name="entry1381994375083931p0"></a>funcs</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry410261431083931p0"><a name="entry410261431083931p0"></a><a name="entry410261431083931p0"></a>输出参数，显示设备控制接口指针，初始化时分配内存，调用者不需要分配内存，调用者获取该指针用于操作显示设备。</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**返回：**

DISPLAY\_SUCCESS 表示执行成功。

其他值表示执行失败，具体错误码查看[DispErrCode](_display.md#ga12a925dadef7573cd74d63d06824f9b0)。

**Since：**

1.0

**Version：**

1.0

## bAlphaMax255<a name="ga17f87b9850f83633f427eeceb74c93a7"></a>

```

## Commit<a name="ga9ba6d2ff58de226e93d71af7aea5df72"></a>

```
int32_t(* DeviceFuncs::Commit) (uint32_t devId, int32_t *fence)
```

**描述：**

提交合成送显请求。

图形服务通过该接口向接口实现层提交合成送显请求，如果有硬件合成层，接口实现层需要在这时进行合成，并且把最终合成的数据送到硬件进行显示。

## GetDisplayCapability<a name="gae570b817a22a1e5ba9c45c6157389a72"></a>

```
int32_t(* DeviceFuncs::GetDisplayCapability) (uint32_t devId, DisplayCapability *info)
```

**描述：**

获取显示设备能力集。

图形服务可以通过该接口获取显示设备具备哪些显示能力。

**参数:**

<a name="table931340616091459"></a>
<table><thead align="left"><tr id="row1917763448091459"><th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.1"><p id="p238046221091459"><a name="p238046221091459"></a><a name="p238046221091459"></a>名称</p>
</th>
<th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.2"><p id="p1169573477091459"><a name="p1169573477091459"></a><a name="p1169573477091459"></a>描述</p>
</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody><tr id="row1491485761091459"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry789881942091459p0"><a name="entry789881942091459p0"></a><a name="entry789881942091459p0"></a>devId</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry922743682091459p0"><a name="entry922743682091459p0"></a><a name="entry922743682091459p0"></a>输入参数，指示需要操作的设备ID。</p>

</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry1947452366091459p0"><a name="entry1947452366091459p0"></a><a name="entry1947452366091459p0"></a>输出参数，设备支持的能力级信息，详情参考 {@DisplayCapability}。</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**返回:**

DISPLAY\_SUCCESS 表示执行成功。

其他值表示执行失败，具体错误码查看[DispErrCode](_display.md#ga12a925dadef7573cd74d63d06824f9b0)。

## GetDisplayCompChange<a name="ga7c2156f6c00f2c61988b2936edb4ce4f"></a>

```
int32_t(* DeviceFuncs::GetDisplayCompChange) (uint32_t devId, uint32_t *num, uint32_t *Layers, int32_t *type)
```

**描述：**

获取显示设备合成类型有变化的layer。

在合成准备阶段，显示设备会根据设备的合成能力修改图层的合成类型，该接口会返回哪些图层合成类型发生了变化。

**参数:**

<a name="table120167083091459"></a>
<table><thead align="left"><tr id="row939221996091459"><th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.1"><p id="p1441019898091459"><a name="p1441019898091459"></a><a name="p1441019898091459"></a>名称</p>
</th>
<th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.2"><p id="p1368149772091459"><a name="p1368149772091459"></a><a name="p1368149772091459"></a>描述</p>
</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody><tr id="row247814656091459"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry1031966971091459p0"><a name="entry1031966971091459p0"></a><a name="entry1031966971091459p0"></a>devId</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry823210370091459p0"><a name="entry823210370091459p0"></a><a name="entry823210370091459p0"></a>输入参数，指示需要操作的设备ID。</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="row1015818237091459"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry803848810091459p0"><a name="entry803848810091459p0"></a><a name="entry803848810091459p0"></a>num</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry20817567091459p0"><a name="entry20817567091459p0"></a><a name="entry20817567091459p0"></a>输出参数，表示合成类型发生了变化的图层数量。</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="row1028172280091459"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry1235869870091459p0"><a name="entry1235869870091459p0"></a><a name="entry1235869870091459p0"></a>Layers</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry1728653299091459p0"><a name="entry1728653299091459p0"></a><a name="entry1728653299091459p0"></a>输出参数，指向图层数组首地址。</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="row433875523091459"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry1503832412091459p0"><a name="entry1503832412091459p0"></a><a name="entry1503832412091459p0"></a>type</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry1515037197091459p0"><a name="entry1515037197091459p0"></a><a name="entry1515037197091459p0"></a>输出参数，指向合成类型数组首地址。</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**返回:**

DISPLAY\_SUCCESS 表示执行成功。

其他值表示执行失败，具体错误码查看[DispErrCode](_display.md#ga12a925dadef7573cd74d63d06824f9b0)。

```

**描述：**

## GetWriteBackFrame<a name="gaaabf8b87f2d7eb1a48c0fc75745eb550"></a>

```
int32_t(* DeviceFuncs::GetWriteBackFrame) (uint32_t devId, BufferHandle *buffer, int32_t *fence)
```

**描述：**

获取显示设备的回写帧。

该接口用来获取devId指定的回写点数据，接口实现层将显示设备回写点的数据写入到设置的缓存中。

**参数:**

<a name="table587230480153217"></a>
<table><thead align="left"><tr id="row842263960153217"><th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.1"><p id="p1570209200153217"><a name="p1570209200153217"></a><a name="p1570209200153217"></a>名称</p>
</th>
<th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.2"><p id="p1275456214153217"><a name="p1275456214153217"></a><a name="p1275456214153217"></a>描述</p>
</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody><tr id="row348233200153217"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry2012321508153217p0"><a name="entry2012321508153217p0"></a><a name="entry2012321508153217p0"></a>devId</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry1291885615153217p0"><a name="entry1291885615153217p0"></a><a name="entry1291885615153217p0"></a>输入参数，指示需要操作的设备ID。</p>
</td>

<tr id="row780885142153217"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry1947596943153217p0"><a name="entry1947596943153217p0"></a><a name="entry1947596943153217p0"></a>buffer</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry1566066597153217p0"><a name="entry1566066597153217p0"></a><a name="entry1566066597153217p0"></a>输出参数，回写点数据缓存。</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="row1917422403153217"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry548988191153217p0"><a name="entry548988191153217p0"></a><a name="entry548988191153217p0"></a>fence</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry139275057153217p0"><a name="entry139275057153217p0"></a><a name="entry139275057153217p0"></a>输出参数，同步栅栏，图形服务在调用该接口时，需要将Buffer的release fence 传入，标记该缓存是否可以被写入，接口实现层在接口返回前需要将buffer的acquirce fence 写入回传给图形服务，用来标记回写数据是否已经写入缓存。</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**返回:**

DISPLAY\_SUCCESS 表示执行成功。

其他值表示执行失败，具体错误码查看[DispErrCode](_display.md#ga12a925dadef7573cd74d63d06824f9b0)。

## SetDisplayVsyncEnabled<a name="gab235d653b12500b4f37325202f2bc98f"></a>

```
int32_t(* DeviceFuncs::SetDisplayVsyncEnabled) (uint32_t devId, bool enabled)
```

**描述：**

使能垂直同步信号。

图形服务可以通过该接口使能或取消垂直同步信号，当有垂直同步信号产生时，接口实现层需要回调图形服务通过RegDisplayVBlankCallback注册的 VBlankCallback 回调。 图形服务在需要刷新显示时需要使能垂直同步信号，在收到VBlankCallback事件回调时再进行合成送显，不需要刷新显示时需要取消垂直同步信号。

**参数:**

<a name="table1688211646091459"></a>
<table><thead align="left"><tr id="row1852311280091459"><th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.1"><p id="p139394080091459"><a name="p139394080091459"></a><a name="p139394080091459"></a>名称</p>
</th>
<th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.2"><p id="p2135046034091459"><a name="p2135046034091459"></a><a name="p2135046034091459"></a>描述</p>
</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody><tr id="row547231929091459"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry1317946783091459p0"><a name="entry1317946783091459p0"></a><a name="entry1317946783091459p0"></a>devId</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry1684820871091459p0"><a name="entry1684820871091459p0"></a><a name="entry1684820871091459p0"></a>输入参数，指示需要操作的设备ID。</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="row150592989091459"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry1201769249091459p0"><a name="entry1201769249091459p0"></a><a name="entry1201769249091459p0"></a>enabled</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry1268357308091459p0"><a name="entry1268357308091459p0"></a><a name="entry1268357308091459p0"></a>输入参数，使能状态，true表示能，false表示不能。</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**返回:**

DISPLAY\_SUCCESS 表示执行成功。

其他值表示执行失败，具体错误码查看[DispErrCode](_display.md#ga12a925dadef7573cd74d63d06824f9b0)。

## SetVirtualDisplayBuffer<a name="gae3d82da3881c5a0a69175a7ee7c7072d"></a>

```
int32_t(* DeviceFuncs::SetVirtualDisplayBuffer) (uint32_t devId, BufferHandle *buffer, int32_t fence)
```

**描述：**

设置虚拟屏的输出缓存。

该接口用于设置虚拟屏输出缓存，接口实现层需要将虚拟屏的输出放入到该缓存中，接口实现层需要等待同步栅栏发送信号后才能使用缓存。

**参数:**

<table><thead align="left"><tr id="row812090456153217"><th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.1"><p id="p282311000153217"><a name="p282311000153217"></a><a name="p282311000153217"></a>名称</p>
</th>
<th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" id="mcps1.1.3.1.2"><p id="p1902932113153217"><a name="p1902932113153217"></a><a name="p1902932113153217"></a>描述</p>
</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody><tr id="row946070824153217"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry714728013153217p0"><a name="entry714728013153217p0"></a><a name="entry714728013153217p0"></a>devId</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry1358240349153217p0"><a name="entry1358240349153217p0"></a><a name="entry1358240349153217p0"></a>输入参数，指示需要操作的设备ID。</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="row318169322153217"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry1215174116153217p0"><a name="entry1215174116153217p0"></a><a name="entry1215174116153217p0"></a>buffer</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry6796817153217p0"><a name="entry6796817153217p0"></a><a name="entry6796817153217p0"></a>输出参数，输出缓存。</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="row499779360153217"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.1 "><p id="entry588219958153217p0"><a name="entry588219958153217p0"></a><a name="entry588219958153217p0"></a>fence</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%" headers="mcps1.1.3.1.2 "><p id="entry609660460153217p0"><a name="entry609660460153217p0"></a><a name="entry609660460153217p0"></a>输出参数，同步栅栏。</p>

**返回:**

DISPLAY\_SUCCESS 表示执行成功。

其他值表示执行失败，具体错误码查看[DispErrCode](_display.md#ga12a925dadef7573cd74d63d06824f9b0)。
